

Chapter 10


The king of the city, the king of the city.

As soon as these words came out, Du Jiang's face changed.

He looked at the extremely confident face in front of him, his face was ashen.

In his opinion, Gao Yang must be a person who seeks fame and reputation. He didn't know what means he used to gain the trust of the empress.

How could the lives of hundreds of thousands of people in a city be so reckless!

Once the people are really living in poverty, what's the use of your life?

Du Jiang made up his mind in his heart that if the situation is out of control, he will take this man down even if he has to fight for this black hat!

Even if the empress is behind him, even if he has overwhelming power!

But in his heart, the lives of the people are above everything else!

Only now, he will see what Gao Yang is going to do!

Gao Yang looked at Du Jiang and said, "Bring the map of Linjiang City."

Du Jiang gave a look, and one of his men quickly brought a map.

The map was spread out on the table, and the geographical location of the entire Linjiang City was clear at a glance.

Gao Yang took a quick look and frowned, "How is the food in Linjiang City generally transported?"

Hearing this question, Du Jiang despised Gao Yang even more in his heart.

He said coldly, "Of course, it is transported by land and water, but Linjiang City is famous for being close to the Qingshui River, so there are more water transportation, which is fast and has less loss."

"Does Mr. Gao have a good plan in mind?"

Du Jiang spoke directly, looking at Gao Yang with a pair of hawk-like eyes.

Gao Yang's fingers passed over the places where the Qingshui River flows one by one, and the corners of his lips curled up slightly.

He did not directly answer Du Jiang's question, but asked, "Does County Magistrate Du know the biggest grain merchants in Linjiang City?"

"The four families of Qian, Zhao, Han, and Lin have been entrenched in Linjiang City for a hundred years and are very powerful. Taking advantage of this disaster, they frantically swept up the grain on the market, causing some local small grain merchants to follow suit and hoard grain, making a fortune in the national crisis!"

"This also caused the grain price in Linjiang City to almost double in just a few dozen days!"

"But now that your majesty has just ascended the throne, the people of Linjiang City are tough and cannot be forced Suppress them, otherwise there will be chaos. At that time, I am afraid that no one can bear the consequences. "

Gao Yang smiled faintly, "Please ask County Magistrate Du to prepare a table of good wine and food for this young master to entertain the four families of Zhao, Han, and Lin!"

Du Jiang shook his head more and more, "Young Master Gao, to be honest, I have used this trick before, but it has little effect. Merchants value profit and seize this God-given opportunity to hoard grain. They will never let go so easily."

"Just do it." Gao Yang said, and walked directly into the government office.

Du Jiang stared at Gao Yang's back, and walked away angrily, "Then I'll see what Young Master Gao can do!"

On the side, Shangguan Wan'er looked at Gao Yang and didn't say anything.

But she was curious in her heart, what exactly Gao Yang wanted to do.

"..."

Linjiang City.

Lin Family.

As a century-old family in Linjiang City, the Lin family mansion has a deep courtyard, with rockeries and water in a staggered manner, like a miniature mountain and river painting.

The pavilion in the center of the lake is located in the center of the pool. It has an octagonal eaves and an antique style. The pavilion is beautifully decorated with carved beams and painted buildings. Carps are vying to jump out, showing the prosperity.

"Mr. Lin, Lord Du has sent news that the court has sent an imperial censor to take over all affairs of Linjiang City. He has specially summoned us to go. I'm afraid it is to reduce the price of grain. What should we do?"

In the pavilion in the center of the lake.

The three middle-aged people are centered around an old man who is wearing a luxurious robe with precious jewels and gold threads on the collar and cuffs.

The head of the Qian family couldn't help but speak with a look of sadness on his face.

Hearing the news, Elder Lin looked calm and said, "What are you afraid of for just attending the banquet?"

"He said to lower the grain price, so we lower the grain price?"

Elder Lin sneered and glanced at the three people: "As long as we work together, Daqian has suffered from natural disasters for many years, and there is not much grain in the grain warehouse in Linjiang City. We will eat as much as the grain in the grain warehouse. Not only will the grain price in Linjiang City not fall, it can rise to 110 coins per bucket!"

"As long as we seize this opportunity, it will be enough for our descendants!"

Hearing this, everyone's eyes showed a trace of greed.

110 coins per bucket, according to the grain they have now, that is a sky-high price of silver!

"Mr. Lin is right. As long as we are united, the empress has just ascended the throne, how dare they force their way in?"

But the head of the Zhao family, who had a big mole on his face, was a little worried. "I heard that the new censor is very young and came from Chang'an. I'm afraid he has a big background. If we don't give him face, what if he gets angry?"

If you are a big shot in Chang'an, I'm afraid you will be annihilated!"

When Elder Lin heard this, his face changed.

But he still said, "The empress ascended the throne, and the world is finally governed by law, but what the head of the Zhao family said makes sense. The arrival of the Supervisory Censor should be given some face."

"Now the price of grain in Linjiang City is 100 coins per bucket. At the dinner later, we will reduce it by 5 coins. This 5 coins is the face given to the Supervisory Censor!"

"But I have said in advance that if anyone blocks my way to wealth, I will never give up."

A sharp light flashed in Elder Lin's eyes.

"What Elder Lin said is right!"

"We will follow Elder Lin's lead. As long as we are determined, the price of grain in Linjiang City will be decided by us! "

The three of them agreed.

A smile appeared in Elder Lin's eyes, and he straightened his slightly wrinkled robe.

"Change into an ordinary robe and come with me to the banquet."

Everyone looked down at the luxurious robes on their bodies, and they were suddenly enlightened.

"What Elder Lin said is very true!"

"It is still Elder Lin who has superb skills!"

"..."

The backyard of the county government office.

Gao Yang sat in the main seat, Shangguan Wan'er and Du Jiang sat on his left and right, and Luluo stood behind him.

The table in front of them was filled with the best wine and meat, with good color, fragrance and taste.

Gao Yang tapped the table with his fingers, slowly and rhythmically.

Du Jiang couldn't help but say, "Mr. Gao, these grain merchants are all old foxes. It is more difficult to get them to lower the price than to kill them. The maximum reduction is five cents!"

"Five cents is their limit! "

Du Jiang stretched out his palm, his expression excited.

"Du County Magistrate, calm down. As the father and mother of a county, if even you are in a panic, how can you stabilize the grain price?"

Gao Yang said lightly. This Du Jiang is a good father and mother, but too impatient.

This time, it can be regarded as a lesson for him.

Du Jiang was suddenly scolded, his face was livid, "Then I will wait and see what Gao Yushi will do!"

At this time, the accompanying soldiers walked in quickly and said, "Your Excellency Yushi, the four heads of the Qian, Zhao, Han and Lin families are here."

"Send!"

Following Gao Yang's voice, the heads of the four major families of Qian, Zhao, Han and Lin walked in soon.

"We greet Gao Yushi!"

"We greet Gao Yushi! "

Several people shouted in unison.

Gao Yang glanced over and couldn't help laughing.

"I've heard that the four major families of Qian, Zhao, Han and Lin have been in Linjiang City for a hundred years. They are well-known wealthy merchants in the vicinity. How come I see them so destitute today?"

Shangguan Wan'er also had a look of disgust. She was obviously wealthy, but she deliberately wore a simple robe that only ordinary people wore.

This intention was too obvious.

But she was also a little worried. Gao Yang's idea of ​​lowering grain prices today might be ruined.

Old Lin bent down and said, "You don't know, Gao Yushi, Linjiang City was hit by heavy rains, and the fertile fields were destroyed, resulting in refugees everywhere. The people have no food to eat. We are really sad."

"During this period, we have been giving out porridge and taking out a large sum of money for disaster relief. Now we are already out of money! "

Seeing Elder Lin speak, the other three heads of the family echoed, "In recent years, Daqian has suffered from natural disasters one after another, and the people have suffered. We are local gentry and are loved by the people. How can we sit back and watch? But after generous donations, we are almost out of ammunition and food!"

"Censor Gao has arrived, and the pressure on us is much less!"

These words made Du Jiang want to walk away in anger.

Too shameless!

The mansions of these families are extremely prosperous, and are not inferior to the Duke's Mansion in Chang'an. There are hundreds of people in the mansion. As long as they take out the stored food, the people of Linjiang City will not be without food!

Shameless!

These merchants are damned!

Du Jiang was about to explode.

But Gao Yang was not angry at all.

He just said lightly, "The four heads of the family are noble and have a heart of compassion for the world. Gao Yang admires them! "

"It's just that this young master was appointed by the empress to take over all the affairs of Linjiang City."

Lin Lao realized something, looked at the other three, and spoke first, "Since the censor has come to Linjiang City, my Lin family must show sincerity and is willing to reduce the price by five cents and sell grain at a loss!"

"The Qian family is the same!"

"The Zhao family is the same!"

"The Han family is the same!"

Several people gritted their teeth and looked like they had suffered a great loss.

Du Jiang was not surprised at all. No one knew the faces of these wealthy businessmen better than him.

Gao Yang shook his head.

"Reduced by five cents?"

Lin Lao looked unhappy. He didn't expect Gao Yang to have such a big appetite.

A bushel of grain was reduced by five cents, which means tens of thousands of taels of silver were wasted!

"Eight cents!"

"What do you think, censor? "

Lin Lao said in a deep voice.

Gao Yang still shook his head.

Hiss!

The faces of the four major grain merchants were extremely ugly!

Gao Yang is forcing them to tear their faces apart!

Du

Jiang looked at Gao Yang with a sneer on his face. This was not much different from what he expected!

He wanted to see what Gao Yang would do!

Just when Elder Lin was about to walk away, Gao Yang said coldly, "I want all the grain in your hands to be raised to 150 wen per dou. Only higher prices are allowed, no lower prices. If anyone dares to sell grain below 150 wen per dou, I will kill him!"


Chapter 11


The price of a dou should not be less than 150 wen per dou.

When these words came out, everyone was stunned.

Lin Lao's beard trembled, and he almost pulled off all the beard on his chin. His wrinkled old face was full of shock.

The other three grain merchants also looked at Gao Yang in astonishment.

For a moment, the whole county government was silent.

Everyone was stunned.

They even forgot to speak.

Because Gao Yang's words were completely beyond their expectations.

Du Jiang was originally prepared to see how Gao Yang would deal with this group of difficult grain merchants and get them to reduce the price by a few more wen.

As a result, Gao Yang had no intention of lowering the price. On the contrary, he directly raised the price of grain.

And in one breath, the price soared from the current 100 wen per dou, which was already unaffordable for many ordinary people, to 150 wen per dou.

Even these merchants were not allowed to sell low-priced grain!

What did Gao Yang want to do? Was he going to starve the people of Linjiang City to death?

Du Jiang was full of anger, but the four major grain merchants were here, and Gao Yang had taken over all the affairs of Linjiang City.

Even if he was dissatisfied, he could not question Gao Yang in front of the four major grain merchants.

Otherwise, it would be a serious crime of contempt for his superiors.

Shangguan Wan'er was also startled, with a pair of beautiful eyes full of confusion.

Didn't they come to Linjiang City to lower the price of grain?

And from the previous test, Gao Yang should know very clearly that this was an assessment from the empress.

It even concerns the entire Dingguo Mansion.

Gao Yang didn't think about how to lower the price of grain, so why did he raise the price of grain?

And it was such a terrifying number!

Shangguan Wan'er couldn't figure it out at all.

She had followed the empress in power for two months and had seen too many officials, some insidious, some vicious, and some upright and impartial.

But it was the first time she had seen an official like Gao Yang who didn't follow the usual path.

Old Lin was shocked, with disbelief in his eyes, "Censor Gao, I may be old and my ears are not working well. What did you just say? You want me to sell grain at a price lower than 150 wen per dou?"

As soon as these words came out, the eyes of the other three heads of the family all looked at Gao Yang.

Gao Yang tapped his fingers slowly on the table, and he smiled faintly, "Is it difficult to understand what I mean?"

"The price of 150 wen per dou, if anyone dares to sell grain at a price lower than this, and I find out, then he will lose his head!"

"Did you hear it clearly this time?"

Seeing Gao Yang's confirmation again, even if they were cunning, they couldn't help but smile.

Unexpectedly, things took a turn for the worse. Gao Yang summoned them here, but he didn't mean to lower the price.

On the contrary, he wanted to raise the price for them, and it was an incredible price!

A full 150 wen per dou!

Behind this terrifying number, there will be a sky-high profit.

Moreover, everyone in Linjiang City knew that most of the grain was controlled by the four families.

The price of grain soared more than doubled, rising to 100 wen per dou.

This made them suffer from infamy.

But this time, it was a hard rule of the county government that grain must be sold at a price higher than 150 wen per dou, so it was not their turn to bear the infamy!

Not only could he make a lot of money, but he didn't have to bear the infamy himself. Old Lin wanted to laugh out loud.

He had lived for most of his life, and there was such a good thing in the world?

But the more ecstatic he was, the calmer he became.

Elder Lin's cloudy old eyes burst into a gleam of light, and he couldn't help but ask, "Master Censor, will this be posted on the notice?"

As Elder Lin said this, the heads of the Qian, Han, and Zhao families all looked at Gao Yang.

Their eyes also flashed with light.

Posting the notice and announcing it to the whole city would be a done deal, otherwise Gao Yang would change his face and they would be the ones to be cheated.

Everyone present was a smart person, so how could they not be cautious?

Gao Yang looked at Elder Lin with deep eyes and nodded, "After this meal, the notice that the price of grain should not be less than 150 wen per bucket will be posted on every street in Linjiang City."

Elder Lin looked at the other three families, and they were completely settled in their hearts.

Today, a huge wealth has come to the four families. If they don't seize it well, they will be ashamed of the century-old foundation laid by their ancestors.

Next, except for Gao Yang who ate heartily, no one else touched their chopsticks during the meal.

But some flattery, in the mouths of Elder Lin and the three heads of the family, is like a torrent of water.

Soon, the four major grain merchants all said goodbye.

"Elder Lin, what is this new censor fighting for?

What is he thinking? He didn't ask us to lower the grain price, but raised the grain price to 150 Wen per bucket. Is there a problem? "

Outside the county government office.

The head of the Qian family couldn't help but say.

Old Lin snorted coldly, "I have lived half my life and have seen all kinds of situations. I have never seen grain prices soar and fall again!"

"No matter what this Gao Yushi has in mind, it has nothing to do with us. Now, we should take advantage of this great opportunity to make a fortune."

"Such a rare opportunity, as long as you seize it, the family will not worry for a hundred years, and no matter how chaotic Linjiang City is, it has nothing to do with us, because we are following the will of the county government!"

"A huge fortune is right in front of you. If you are still hesitant, you are really stupid!"

As soon as these words came out, the head of the Qian family apologized quickly, "Old Lin, calm down. It's just that I have lived half my life and have never seen such a good thing, so I am a little worried. "

"But according to what Elder Lin said, this is really a huge fortune."

"My Qian family only follows Elder Lin's lead!"

The heads of the Zhao and Han families also said, "The four major families in Linjiang City have always advanced and retreated together. Whatever Elder Lin wants to do next, we will definitely follow."

When Elder Lin heard what they said, he looked at the pedestrians on the streets of Linjiang City with a deep gaze, and his turbid old eyes burst out with endless greed.

"Take advantage of the fact that the county government's notice has not been posted yet, and quickly sweep up all the grain on the market in Linjiang City at a price of 100 coins per bucket!"

"Then wait for the grain price to skyrocket. Once the county government's notice is released, the grain price will never be only 150 coins per bucket. In troubled times, the grain price is too high, and the people can't survive. No matter how high the price of grain is, they will sell their pots and irons to buy it! "

Lin Lao's voice was chilling.

Let alone 150 wen per dou, even if the price of grain breaks through 100 wen per dou, Linjiang City will be full of starving people, and thousands and tens of thousands of people will starve to death!

Let alone 150 wen per dou, or even higher, it will only take ten days or half a month, it will be a real hell on earth.

But whether it is Lin Lao or the other three grain merchants, they all have no expression on their faces, and there is only greed in their eyes!

What does the life and death of the people have to do with them?

In such a chaotic world, for them, seizing the opportunity and making a fortune in national disasters is the kingly way!

Linjiang City, the price of grain will usher in an incredible surge!

"..."

Inside the county government.

Du Jiang looked at Gao Yang with disbelief, "Gao Yushi, are you really going to post the notice that the price of grain cannot be sold at less than 150 wen per dou all over Linjiang City? "

Du Jiang's face was full of anger. He thought Gao Yang must be crazy.

It would be fine if he said this to the four major grain merchants, but he actually posted a notice all over Linjiang City.

Once the notice is out, there will be no room for maneuver!

Even if this notice is out, the Linjiang County Government will become the target of public criticism, and the angry saliva of the people can spray them to death!

What's more, isn't their goal to lower the price of grain?

Why did Gao Yang raise the price of grain, and it was a sky-high price!

After a long while, Gao Yang slowly looked at Du Jiang, "Master Du, do as I say."

"Others are not what you should ask. "

Gao Yang's eyes were cold.

Du Jiang trembled all over, his eyes staring at Gao Yang, his heart ached, the empress had a great reputation, but why did she send such a shameless person.

Does he know what the price of grain is 150 wen a dou?

Why not eat meat porridge!

This is why not eat meat porridge!

The only word left in Du Jiang's mind, how could the children of big figures in Chang'an City, who were born with a golden key, know the suffering of ordinary people?

This is a disaster for Linjiang City, and it is also a disaster for countless people!

But Du Jiang still wants to work hard, so he is the parent official of hundreds of thousands of people in Linjiang City, and he must live up to the black hat on his head!

He asked word by word, "Sir, do you know the consequences of doing this?"

"Once the notice is published, within ten days or half a month, Linjiang City will definitely be a purgatory on earth, countless people will starve to death, and even their wives and children will be separated, and it is not impossible to exchange their children for food! "

Du Jiang gritted his teeth and knelt on one knee, "I have been over 36 years old since I was born. I am proud and have never asked anyone for help. But today, I beg you to take back your order. The price of grain has reached 150 coins per bucket. Except for merchants, ordinary people can't afford it!"

Gao Yang looked at Du Jiang, his eyes did not fluctuate at all.

He knew that Du Jiang was a parent official who was dedicated to the people. After returning to Beijing this time, he would also report to promote Du Jiang.

But if Linjiang City wants to lower the price of grain, it must do as he says.

The county government has ears behind the walls. Before he is absolutely sure, he must not say his intentions!

He can only remind Du Jiang, "Master Du, if you want to lower the price of grain, don't

We must try our best to keep food prices down. It should be noted that the more powerful the spring suppresses, the more terrifying the rebound will be! "

"After seven days, everything will be fine!"

"This young master will not joke with his life."

After saying that, Gao Yang walked straight away from the county government office.

After eating and drinking, he still had business to attend to.

Today in Daqian, Linjiang City is not the only city that has been hit by heavy rains. The entire 16th city of Guangyang County has suffered a major disaster.

However, the disaster in Linjiang City was the most severe.

If one move affects the whole body, countless people are destined to be displaced.

Reducing food prices is only one of them.

The most important thing now is to allow people to survive the disaster and even make money!

What should he do?

Gao Yang stood at the door of the inner courtyard of the government office, looked out, and fell into thinking.

Behind him, Du Jiang was so angry that he was shaking all over.

It's hard for him to understand!

He, Du Jiang, has been in power for twelve years and has seen many methods, but he has never heard of methods that can lower food prices by raising food prices!

This is an arrogant lunatic who doesn't understand anything.

He will definitely pay a heavy price!

Before Du Jiang could recover, he heard Gao Yang's voice.

"Master Du, please show me around. I see that this government office has been in disrepair for a long time. When the price of food drops in a few days, it can be renovated."

When Du Jiang heard this, his eyes changed drastically.

The people can no longer survive, so Gaoyang actually wants to renovate the government office?

How is this different from common people?

But before he could speak, Gao Yang took Luluo and walked out of the government office first.

"Sir Shangguan, do you really want to sit back and watch the people of Linjiang City live in poverty?" Du Jiang placed his last hope on Shangguan Wan'er.

Shangguan Wan'er is a popular person around the empress. As long as Shangguan Wan'er takes action, all this can be stopped!

Shangguan Wan'er stared at the direction Gao Yang was leaving, with confusion appearing on her beautiful face.

If it were anyone else, she, Shangguan Wan'er, would definitely stop him.

But this person happened to be Gao Yang, and his monkey game in the Jinluan Palace started completely out of step with common sense.

Is Gao Yang a dandy?

Judging from the past, Gaoyang, the grandson of Duke Dingguo, was not only a playboy, but also a complete bastard.

But he didn't act like a fool.

He should be very aware of the embarrassing situation facing Duke Dingguo.

Shangguan Wan'er's beautiful face flashed with determination, "Her Majesty the Empress has ordered that all affairs in Linjiang City be handed over to Master Gao!"

"But if the situation is urgent and out of control, I will take action to stop it!"

After saying that, Shangguan Wan'er also strode away.

After Du Jiang heard these words, he said sadly, "I'm afraid it will be too late by then!"

"Your Majesty must be informed of this matter as quickly as possible. If he continues to act like this, the hundreds of thousands of people in Linjiang City will be doomed!"

Du Jiang's eyes were firm and he shouted outside, "Take my pen and ink, and I will report it all night long. I will impeach this officer as soon as possible in eight hundred miles!"


Chapter 12


Two days later.

"Report!"

"Eight hundred miles of urgent news from Linjiang City!"

Accompanied by a voice, the guards in black armor hurried into the palace, and then knelt down and raised a memorial.

"Linjiang City?"

"Eight hundred miles of urgent news?"

Wu Zhao wore a golden dragon robe, and her phoenix eyes were full of majesty. When she heard the name of Linjiang City, her brows suddenly relaxed.

"Present it!"

Wu Zhao put down the memorial she was reviewing, and a rare smile hung on her face.

Linjiang City, this is Gao Yang's territory.

Even though a few days had passed, Wu Zhao couldn't help being shocked when she thought of Gao Yang's casual monkey trick in the Golden Palace.

It was incredible that such a vicious trick appeared on the grandson of the Duke of Dingguo from a military family.

Therefore, she was looking forward to Gao Yang's methods in Linjiang City!

But when Wu Zhao opened the memorial, her face changed again and again.

In the end, even her beautiful face was full of anger: "This Gao Yang dared to collude with officials and businessmen to raise grain prices. Not only did he not let local grain merchants lower prices, but he also sold grain at a high price. It's simply unreasonable!"

Just when Wu Zhao was about to give an order, she suddenly paused.

"No!"

"This Gao Yang doesn't look like a mediocre person. Could he have other intentions?"

Wu Zhao frowned. She never expected that Gao Yang would give her such a big surprise.

To be precise, it should be a shock.

She looked at the memorial again, her eyes fell on the characters of Du Jiang's words Gao Yang brazenly said that he would suddenly reduce the grain price in Jiangcheng within seven days.

"On the one hand, you want to reduce the grain price in Jiangcheng, and on the other hand, you want to raise the grain price in Linjiangcheng to a sky-high price. Gao Yang, Gao Yang, what are you going to do?"

"You will cause trouble for me," Wu Zhao sat on the dragon chair and rubbed her eyebrows.

The morning court tomorrow will not be peaceful.

Duke Dingguo is a big tree that attracts the wind. There are too many people in this court who want him to fall.

According to the rules of Daqian, this impeachment will be sent to her imperial study and the Imperial Censorate.

Tomorrow is destined to be a storm!

"..."

The next day, a ray of golden sunlight pierced through the dense dark clouds in the sky and enveloped the entire Chang'an.

Daqian Palace.

Jinluan Palace.

Wu Zhao sat high on the dragon chair, her eyebrows were cold, and a sense of majesty permeated her body.

Civil and military officials lined up on both sides.

Wu Zetian knew that undercurrents were surging in the calm court.

"Your Majesty, I impeach Gao Yang, the son of Duke Dingguo!"

"Gao Yang was highly valued by Your Majesty and was the censor of Linjiang City, but he colluded with officials and businessmen and ordered that the price of grain in Linjiang City should not be lower than 150 wen per bucket, and he also wanted to renovate the government office on a large scale. This move is really stupid. I ask Your Majesty to order severe punishment to serve as an example!"

At the Censorate, an old man with a straight body and gray hair came forward. His face was livid and he was full of righteousness.

The Censor, Yan Zheng, was upright and incorruptible. If he didn't like anything, he would criticize him from top to bottom. No one dared not to criticize him.

Even if it was one of the three regents left by the previous emperor after his death, Prince Rong Wulong dared to impeach him in public!

Prince Rong was so angry that he was sick in the house for the past two days and didn't even come to the morning court.

As he came forward, everyone's face changed.

If Yan Zheng impeached, then the impeached person would be punished.

Gao Feng's eyes widened, and he felt like he was hit hard when he heard this.

Gao Yang's officials and businessmen colluded to manipulate grain prices, and ordered that the grain price in Linjiang City should not be less than 150 coins per bucket?

Didn't he tell Gao Yang that if he couldn't do it, he shouldn't show off. The Duke of Dingguo's Mansion was a lean camel that was bigger than a horse, and it would always be able to save him.

Gao Feng's face changed.

After being shocked, all the officials fell into a huge disagreement.

Wang Zhong, wearing armor, spoke first, "One hundred and fifty coins per dou, if this continues for a long time, it will cause great public outrage, and even starvation everywhere, and hell on earth!"

"I agree with Doctor Yan, please punish severely!"

Minister of Rites Cui Li sneered, and he also stood up and said in a deep voice, "Guangyang County has suffered severe rainstorm disasters during this period. The people have no harvest and it is difficult to survive the disaster year. If such high grain prices are ignored, it may arouse great public outrage!"

"Please stop it in time, Your Majesty, to avoid irreversible consequences!"

For a while, all officials agreed.

"I second the motion!"

"I second the motion!"

Gao Feng's face was ashen and cold.

He couldn't help but look at Wu Zhao. At that moment, only the empress could make the final decision!

Wu Zhao swept her eyes over the ministers, took a deep breath and said, "

The grandson of Duke Dingguo is not an ordinary person. Since I have promised, he has extraordinary talents and must be treated by extraordinary people. It has only been two days. Why are you anxious, my dear ministers? "

"Maybe the grandson of Duke Dingguo will hand in a satisfactory answer!"

Wu Zhao swept her eyes over the ministers, and her powerful majesty forced them to bow their heads.

But Wang Zhong sneered subconsciously, "If you want the grain price to fall, how can you raise the grain price to the sky?"

"This Gao Yang is an incompetent person, how can he take on such a great task? !"

Wu Zhao's eyes were cold and her voice was cold: "General Wang, are you questioning my vision?"

Wang Zhong panicked and cold sweat oozed from his forehead.

"I have no such intention!"

Wu Zhao swept her eyes over everyone and fell on Yan Zheng, "Linjiang City will not be in chaos, I have already arranged a backup plan! "

"Since County Magistrate Du said that Gao Yang, the grandson of Duke Dingguo, was talking nonsense and that the grain price should be lowered within seven days, then give him seven days. I have made up my mind on this matter and there is no need to say more!"

"..."

The Mansion of the Minister of Rites.

Song Li laughed, "It is easy to tell whether Gao Yang is a dragon or a worm. Thanks to the Empress's trust, it seems that my Song family is right to cancel the engagement."

Song Qingqing heard the news and asked curiously, "Father, is there any news from Linjiang City?"

Song Li nodded, "Yes, Gao Yang went to Linjiang City, and the first thing he did was to summon the four major grain merchants in Linjiang City. Not only did he not think about lowering the grain price, he also strictly ordered the four major grain merchants not to sell grain at a price lower than 150 Wen per bucket."

"Today, the impeachment memorials have all arrived at the Golden Palace. If it were not for the Empress's strong protection, Gao Yang would have been in trouble! "

After hearing this, Song Qingqing's face showed no expression.

She shook her head and said, "Gao Yang is really confused. Fortunately, my Song family broke off the engagement in advance, otherwise we would inevitably be implicated."

"Merchants are greedy. Instead of lowering the price of grain, he raised it up. If these greedy grain merchants don't raise the price of grain to a sky-high level, I, Song Li, might as well kill myself with a piece of tofu!"

Song Li looked disdainful and took a sip of tea.

Then, he said to Song Qingqing earnestly, "Cui Zhuangyuan went to Qingshui City and Gao Yang went to Linjiang City. The disasters in the two places are similar. It is obviously a competition!"

"But in this competition, Gao Yang is doomed to fail miserably. Cui Zhuangyuan will become the most eye-catching figure in the whole Chang'an and is destined to soar to the sky. Qingqing, you must seize the opportunity. "

Song Qingqing smiled faintly, "Don't worry, father. Mr. Cui is very talented and charming. My daughter has already met him. Mr. Cui should have a good impression of my daughter."

Song Li was surprised and couldn't help stroking his beard, saying, "If we can win Mr. Cui, my Song family will prosper!"


Chapter 13


The old man was buried in the grave, and the old man was buried.

Qingshui City.

Cui Xinghe stood in the government office with his hands behind his back, holding an envelope that was sent from Chang'an at the fastest speed.

This Cui Zhuangyuan is really amazing.

He had only been in Qingshui City for one day, and he used thunderous means to directly reduce the prices of the major grain merchants in Qingshui City by five cents!

The grain price in Qingshui City dropped from 100 wen to 95 wen. Then, the next day, the government ordered the opening of the warehouses to release grain. At the same time, the government purchased grain from the market and reduced the grain price by another 5 wen at the price of 90 wen per dou!

The grain price in the market stabilized at 90 wen per dou.

Such measures impressed the county magistrate of Qingshui City. He heard that the grain price in Linjiang City not far away was not curbed, but on the contrary, it began to soar...

After reading the letter in his hand, Cui Xinghe showed a hint of disdain on his handsome face.

Then he said directly, "The people of Linjiang City are miserable!"

Behind him, the magistrate of Qingshui City asked curiously, "Cui Yushi, what happened? Why are the people of Linjiang City miserable?"

Cui Xinghe looked back at the magistrate of Qingshui City and said calmly, "Gao Yang, the grandson of Duke Dingguo, arrived in Linjiang City. The first order he issued was to order the four major grain merchants in Linjiang City not to sell grain at a price lower than 150 wen per dou!"

"150 wen per dou?"

"What?"

This price is enough to kill the people!

Cui Xinghe said with disdain.

He thought of the empress's arrangement and felt ridiculous.

He, Cui Xinghe, is a descendant of a famous family. Daqian has suppressed all the students in the world.

How can his knowledge and strategy be compared with a waste who can only play vicious tricks?

And by comparison, Linjiang City is more serious.

This was a great shame in Cui Xinghe's eyes!

Gao Yang was a playboy, spending his days in Chang'an, while Cui Xinghe was devoted to studying statecraft in the Hanlin Academy. However, in the heart of the empress, Gao Yang was more important.

This was a shame for the entire Cui family, and even more so for Cui Xinghe!

Thinking of this, Cui Xinghe's eyes became colder.

"Pass this censor's order and tell these grain merchants not to be too greedy, otherwise they will anger this censor and it will be a bad ending!"

"The grain price in Qingshui City must be reduced by another eight cents. At eighty-two cents a bucket, they can still make money. It's enough!"

"If you give this censor face, when this censor returns to Chang'an and becomes the secretary of the empress, this censor will still remember this favor. If not, then we can do whatever we want, but I'm afraid they can't afford the price!"

The county magistrate of Qingshui City was surprised when he heard this, "Mr. Cui wants to reduce it by another eight cents?"

In this way, the grain price in Qingshui City will only be eighty-two cents a bucket, although it is still much higher than the previous fifty cents a bucket.

But the people can still afford it if they grit their teeth and tighten their belts. At least it won't be a purgatory scene with starving people everywhere.

Of course, in such a disaster year, a job to support a family is too precious. For the poor people, even if the price is reduced to 50 wen per dou, they will still starve to death!

In the eyes of the magistrate of Qingshui City, this is already hard-won.

Cui Xinghe nodded, "I have secretly investigated the grain prices in Qingshui River and made a statistics. The two major grain merchants Liu and Tian are almost hoarding grain at a price of 53 wen to 71 wen, not to mention that they still have last year's old grain in their mansion!"

"At 82 wen per dou, they still have a profit, and they will not be ruined."

"Officials should relax and tighten, and give sweet dates after a stick, which is the way to govern the country!"

The magistrate of Qingshui City admired him very much.

"Yushi Cui is a great talent. On behalf of more than 50,000 people in Qingshui City, I would like to thank Yushi Cui!"

"Daqian has Yushi Cui, which is a blessing for the country!"

After saying that, the Qingshui City County Magistrate immediately went down to deliver the message.

After the two major grain merchants in Qingshui City heard Cui Xinghe's message, they all fell silent.

On the one hand, there is a good relationship between the Cui family of Chang'an and the number one scholar of Daqian. On the other hand, the two sides are at odds with each other and use their own methods.

But Cui Xinghe left another way for them.

With a food price of eighty-two cents, you can still make a lot of money.

Under this kind of game.

Soon, food prices in Qingshui City dropped again!

It was just declining in a slow manner, so that he could make more money, but Cui Xinghe didn't care about it.

A sudden reduction of eight cents will cause food prices to fluctuate too much and fall slowly. The two companies will not only be able to better control food prices, but also make more money.

After doing all this, Cui Xinghe looked towards the north of Qingshui City with a chill in his eyes.

"On one side is the sudden drop of eighteen cents in Qingshui City, and on the other side is the one hundred and fifty cents per dou in Linjiang City, or even higher food prices."

"I, Cui Xinghe, am destined to shine throughout Chang'an!"

Linjiang City.

Wave after wave of sound spread far away, making Du Jiang in the county government look sad.

The master replied, "It should be at Huaguo Temple!"

Du Jiang's expression changed, "Go to the temple again?"

His face was ashen.

During these seven days, Gao Yang, in addition to ordering major grain merchants not to sell grain for less than one hundred and fifty coppers per dou, other than that, he either went to Qingshui River to play or went to temples to worship Buddha!

They even want to renovate the county government office and hold large-scale events!

With such laissez-faire behavior, can the price of food in Linjiang City be reduced?

"The seven-day period has arrived. I will go to see Mr. Gao now to see how the price of the food he guaranteed with his life can be reduced!"

"..."

Outside Huaguo Temple.

Throughout Daqian, from dignitaries to ordinary people, countless people burned incense and worshiped Buddha.

After Gao Yang burned a few sticks of incense, he was personally sent out by the abbot of Huaguo Temple.

The two chatted happily.

This scene made Du Jiang, who came to find Gao Yang, gnash his teeth angrily.

He does not believe in Buddhism at all. In his heart, if there are really gods and Buddhas everywhere in the world, he can hear the sufferings of the common people.

Then how could there be so many catastrophes in this world?

The gods and Buddhas in the sky are all a joke!

When the host entered the temple, Du Jiang couldn't help but ask, "Gao Yushi, seven days have passed!"

"But the price of food in Linjiang City has not dropped. On the contrary, it has been rising all the way. Since your decree, the price of food has soared to one hundred and fifty cents per dou. Not only that, it has continued to rise, reaching a full two hundred cents. After a fight, since the county government posted the notice, people outside the county government are pleading for help every day! "

"If this continues, the situation will get out of control and everything will be too late by then. Are you really not afraid?"

Du Jiang said with despair.

He originally wanted to report it to the Empress quickly, hoping that the Empress would stop his ridiculous behavior, but not only did nothing happen, but he also got the Empress to act according to her orders!

And he also made inquiries and finally learned Gao Yang's identity.

Grandson of Gao Tianlong, Duke of Dingguo, a famous dandy in Chang'an

.

After the news came, he collapsed in a chair in despair, and didn't come back to his senses for a long time.

In the next few days, Gao Yang strictly ordered the county government's granary not to open the warehouse to release grain, and then began to wander around.

Either he took him to the Qingshui River that runs through the entire Guangyang County to enjoy the scenery, or he went to the temple every day to pray and chat with the host, just like a believer.

Gao Yang went to more than a dozen temples near Linjiang City!

Seeing that seven days had passed, the grain price in Linjiang City not only did not drop, but on the contrary it went up all the way, even far higher than the 150 wen per dou on the county government's list, reaching a terrifying 200 wen per dou!

Moreover, there was still a rising trend.

Gao Yang not only did not use any means to curb it, but on the contrary he wanted to take advantage of this disaster to renovate the government office and hold large-scale events!

Therefore, even though he knew that Gao Yang was confused, he couldn't help but remind Gao Yang, hoping that he would think of a way.

If this continues, a big chaos will come in Linjiang City!

Gao Yang looked at Du Jiang, without giving a direct answer, but said indifferently: "What have the four major grain merchants done in the past few days?"

Du Jiang said with a gloomy face, "Since the county government posted the notice, the four major grain merchants have used a large amount of money to frantically sweep up the grain in the hands of other small grain merchants at a price of 100 coins per bucket. They will not sell even if it is 150 coins per bucket, causing the grain price to rise all the way. Now they are hoarding grain and waiting for the people to run out of food, and then continue to raise the grain price!"

"These people won't even sell it for 200 coins per bucket!"

Gao Yang smiled, his eyes cold, "Tomorrow, we will recruit workers to start renovating the government office, and post a notice to the public. I will hold a grand dragon boat race!"

"The winner can be exempted from commercial taxes for three years!"


Chapter 14

As soon as these words came out.

Buzz!

Foreign grain merchants!

Even the pretty face of Lu Luo, her plump breasts kept rising and falling.

"In Linjiang City, the number of foreign grain merchants is increasing every day. Linjiang City is no longer short of grain now."

"These merchants want to make a fortune in the national crisis. This time, I will make them destroy their families!"

Qin Yu's eyes showed a coldness. His voice was not loud, but Du Jiang and Shangguan Wan'er heard it very clearly.

Chapter 16

There is no harm without comparison.

Linjiang City and Qingshui City are connected by a Qingshui River, only dozens of miles away.

The grain price in Linjiang City was as high as 220 Wen per dou!

Such a gap was simply unacceptable to the people.

Corrupt official, Gao Baipi, these are all nicknames for Gao Yang.

Linjiang City is about to explode!

This article is basically some historical and modern vicious schemes and methods, but it is integrated into the fictional ancient times, so the background is fictional, reshaping a world, but there will be some shadows of various dynasties.

1: The idea of ​​destroying the whole family and the monkey game come from the Internet. The monkey game comes from the Ming Dynasty. It is also called the Thousand Doors and Seventy-two Grounds Game on the Internet. It is a means of setting up a game, burying gold in the barren mountains.

2: Raising food prices, using work instead of relief, and tourism to stimulate consumption are from Fan Zhongyan of the Northern Song Dynasty, named Three Strategies for Famine Control.

3: The means of locust extermination refer to the means of locust extermination in modern and ancient times, and refer to a series of materials such as CNKI, such as the East Asian migratory locust, such as the swarm The papers on living and solitary types, biological control, etc., refer to the superstition of Li Shimin of the Tang Dynasty eating locusts, as well as Yao Chong's extermination of a major locust plague during the Kaiyuan period of the Tang Dynasty, Su Shi's extermination of locusts in the Song Dynasty, and the modern way of eating locusts.

Fourth, the art of war is a way for Mongolia to conquer the world, slaughter a few, then surround a few, and then Wenhe and Zhongde.

When lye is added to lard, a saponification reaction will occur.

Caustic soda is more difficult to handle, but it can be replaced by wood ash in the stove pit.

Gao Yang showed a smile that made Shangguan Wan'er's heart tremble, and he continued, "Not only do I have some research on merchants and the art of war, I also have some research on the direction of the Daqian River!"

"It's just that this strategy requires much more manpower than building the Ling Canal, but once it succeeds, the sword will be placed on the necks of Chu and Dayan."

For a moment, all the officials' eyes were focused on Gao Yang.

"The terrain of Dagan is higher in the west and lower in the east. Most rivers flow from west to east, such as the Yellow River, Yangtze River, Huaihe River and other rivers, but there are also rivers flowing in other directions."

"The Canglan River flows all the way south, while the Brahmaputra River in our Dagan Plateau area first flows east and then south."

"South of Daqian is the State of Chu and Yan. There are often droughts and water shortages in the two countries. The main rivers in their territory have just changed their names. Half of their water is the water of the Canglan River and the Yarlung Zangbo River in our Dagan. ”

"If we can cut off the water flow from the Yarlung Zangbo River and the Lancang River and divert the water into the source of the Yangtze River and the Yellow River, not only will we be able to gain more than 10,000 acres of fertile farmland, but we will also be able to cut off the water flow in Dachu and Yan, which will definitely become drier, and if we want to It’s just a thought to make him suffer from floods!”

"I wonder what you think of this plan?"

One word fell.

The entire Jinluan Palace fell into deathly silence for an instant, and everyone's eyes widened in disbelief.

Wu Zhao also clenched his fists and his beautiful eyes widened.

Shangguan Wan'er almost lost her balance and fell to the ground.

Da Chu and Yan have been suffering from drought all year round. If Da Gan can cut off the Canglan River and Brahmaputra River, they can hang a knife on the necks of Da Chu and Yan.

Even man-made floods!

Cui Xinghe's face trembled wildly, and he looked at where Gao Yang was in horror. All the court officials, including Gao Feng and Gao Tianlong, looked shocked.

Is this a plan proposed by people?

He said that building the Lingqu canal would waste people and money, but it would block the water of a river and change its course.

When it comes to the Yellow River and the Yangtze River, isn't this project ten times as majestic?

Wouldn’t this be more wasteful for people and money?

Cui Xinghe originally thought that Gao Yang was really a conservative, but he didn't expect that he was a conservative who thought the radicals were too conservative!

If this is really done, the end of Da Chu and Da Yan will come. Even in a single thought, the people of Da Chu and Da Yan will be miserable and wail everywhere!

Wu Zhao's eyes moved, and his phoenix eyes became brighter and brighter.

As soon as Gao Yang saw Wu Zhao's expression, he knew that Wu Zhao was tempted.

But Cui Xinghe came back to his senses and said decisively, "This is absolutely impossible!"

"Not to mention the Canglan River and the Yarlung Zangbo River, whether our current national strength alone can cut them off and lead them to the source of the Yangtze and Yellow Rivers, even if it is successful, there will be a cost that our Dagan cannot afford. cost!"

"Furthermore, once this large-scale project is started, it will definitely not be hidden from Da Chu and Da Yan. They will definitely send their troops to fight. Otherwise, the two countries will really have my Da Gan sword hanging around their necks!"

"War is coming in an instant!"

"Although it will have great benefits after it is completed, the price mentioned by Mr. Gao is also too high."

Lu Zhen and other military generals kept saying, "A bunch of old men, everything depends on human effort. Isn't it possible that people won't die if they repair the Ling Canal?"

"You guys are really impressive, this is just the difference between more deaths and less deaths!"

"I support the clever plan of the household minister Wai Lang. Rather than having a knife hanging over my own head, it is better to place the knife on someone else's neck!"

For a moment, there was a commotion in the Jinluan Hall.

But Gao Yang, the instigator, is still there.

Poisoners, just come up with poisonous plans. Whether it is feasible or not is a matter for Wu Zhao and the officials.

When Wu Zhao came back to his senses, he also felt that this matter was too fantastic.

But this quarrel was able to delay the matter, which actually achieved her goal.

"Enough!"

As soon as her voice came out, all the officials immediately fell silent.

Wu Zhao looked at the officials and said, "The world is currently stable. For me, Dagan, it is not appropriate to waste people and money."

"Let me think carefully about this matter. A member of the Ministry of Revenue, Wai Lang, will come with me and retreat from the court!"

After Wu Zhao finished speaking, he stood up!

"yes!"

"With your help, I will definitely create a hegemonic career."

Wu Zhao came back to his senses. There was no flaw in the slightest, and his noble face was filled with thrilling beauty under the golden sunlight.

Gao Yang said with a puzzled expression, "Your Majesty, where did I mess up the situation?"
